      def convert2(ashmira):
          L=[]
          count=0
          for i in  ast.literal_eval(ashmira):
              if count<3:
                   L.append(i['name'])
                   count=count+1
              else:
                  break
          return L

      def convert4(ashmira):
          L=[]
          for i in  ast.literal_eval(ashmira):
              if i['job']=='Director':
                  L.append(i['name'])
                  break
          return L

      import nltk
      from nltk.stem.porter import PorterStemmer
      ps= PorterStemmer()
      def stem(text):
          y=[]
          for i in text.split():
              y.append(ps.stem(i))
          return " ".join(y)

      def recommend(movie):
          movie_index=new_df[new_df['title']==movie].index[0]
          distaces=similarity[movie_index]
          movies_list=sorted(list(enumerate( distaces)),reverse=True,key=lambda x:x[1])[1:6]   
          
          for i in movies_list:
                  print(new_df.iloc[i[0]].title)
